class=\"clearboth\"></div></div></div><div><span class=\"icon log\"></span><span class=\"count\"></span><pre class=\"text\"></pre></div>"],"text":["In 6 scenes,model has made 2,4,4,0,6,11 mistakes respectively.. The 5th example is extreme overfit because all heads are predicted to come from one coin and the tail from another because of high switching probability and higher probability of showing head in one than the other and this trait led to a lot of errors(6).Also high difference between the probability of showing heads in two coins infact helps the model to predict better, the last example shows how bad the model performs(11 errors)with equal head probability and examples with higher difference between probability of showing head tends to perform better. Besides,lower switching probability lead to underfit and higher switching probability leads to overfit. ","From the first two graphs, it is evident how setting high coin switching probability led the model to extremely overfit and error-prone.Both of the scenes have a coin with high head probability and the coin switching probability is high too,so everytime the model sees head, it predicts that this head came from the coin with high head probability and tail came from the other coin. This way the model became really overfitting since it completely ignores that a face can come from a low likelihood place too.Thus this model sees spurious pattern and made 4 errors in each case. Low switching probability can make a model error-prone since no matter what face comes, it predicts the same coin up to some certain and example3 has made 7 mistakes in this way.","The model kinda fits human's response but not that greatly.Peaks and troughs of human data graph are sharper because subjects actually chose probability from a set of particular probabilities(because they just gave a rating and we did calculation later for finding probability)but the peaks and troughs are more continuous and smoother in the model because it doesn't have any such constraint.Also human beings are more observant of spurious patterns and tend to take decisions even based on small changes which also lead to these rough transitions in graphs.Also it makes sense to compare with averaged ratings instead of single ratings because single ratings show more overfit and more rough transition of peaks and troughs and averaging the probabilities over multiple people decreases this fact","Setting the coin switch probability impacts the model a lot. From the above graphs and examples in other parts, we see that setting a lower switch probability makes the model to predict the same coin upto a certain extent and the graph has fewer peaks and troughs and thus make mistakes. Again, setting a higher switching probability is erroneous because when it sees a face, it predicts the coin with higher probability of showing that face for that turn which is apparently not the case a lot of times. Again if the probability of showing head is equal for both coins, prediction also becomes hard.","There are cases when predicting coins is hard for both model and human.When probability of showing head is equal in both coins, it is hard for both model and human to predict which coin is showing that regardless of switching probability. For sequence [HTHTHTHT] shown in last graph of (c),given the parameters I mentioned in part(c), human can easily predict that all faces are generated by the fair coin and that is the correct prediction but the model is having a hard time generating the truth and it has made errors half of the time. This kind of scenarios are systematically hard for the model because the model keeps giving repetitive pattern given a repetitive sequence but the coins can be really different to that.In some cases like above,human beings will do better but sometimes they wont"," The HMM is actually not great to model the way people approach this task. As the example I showed in last part, there are sequences which will lead human to predict coins with utmost certainty but not the model and model and human predictions differ a lot.Again there are cases when human are quickly overfitting but the model is having smoother transitions and not overfitting and predicting better.",""],"savedAt":"10/31/2020 1:17:36 AM"}
